  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_00cd71c2-551b-436c-b6a7-02cc38f0d471'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

Along the way, the two dominants may find that submitting to one another uncovers not just a deadly conspiracy, but a passion so raw that it'll leave them both branded by fire...</span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28967089-jessica-s-totally-over-the-top-book-obsession?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28967089-jessica-s-totally-over-the-top-book-obsession?shelf=liked-audiobook-version">liked-audiobook-version</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28967089-jessica-s-totally-over-the-top-book-obsession?shelf=listened-to-on-audio">listened-to-on-audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28967089-jessica-s-totally-over-the-top-book-obsession?shelf=own-book">own-book</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1559704409" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10672901215097643075">Branded by Fire was a good read, but at times Mercy annoyed me. She would act a little bitchy at times and go on and on about how she was a dominant female. Blah blah blah if I had to hear about her dominant ass one more time I would have ripped my hair out. Just saying I get it she is a dominant female and they are hard to mate. Riley was a saint for putting up with Mercy's ass. He was sexy, at times very sweet, protective and supportive! Riley made the book for me. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

And above all since they do not like submitting?<br/><br/><i>“Not so fast are we, wolfie?”<br/>“I was trying,” he said, blocking her next set of blows with his arms, “not to hurt you.”<br/>“I’m not a frickin’ princess”</i><br/><br/>Since there are no Alpha unmated </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_36760114" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/36760114" />
    <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"><img alt=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1403239075p2/1570669.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/36760114?book_show_action=true">Nov 02, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"> Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of complex paranormal romance, Werewolf/shifter fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=shapeshifter">shapeshifter</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=werewolf">werewolf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=kickbutt-heroine">kickbutt-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=futuristic">futuristic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=flawed-heroine">flawed-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=favorite-or-autobuy-author">favorite-or-autobuy-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=hero-in-pursuit">hero-in-pursuit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=hot-and-steamy-romance">hot-and-steamy-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer36760114" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15092719236241567857">Before I wrote a review on this book, I had to sleep on it. I was trying to figure out a way to express my feelings about Mercy. She annoyed the crap out of me for the majority of this book. I felt so bad about it. I love strong women. I am definitely a reader who wants a strong, independent heroine in a story, yet I like the sweet heroines as well. I just like well-written heroines. Mercy was certainly well-written. I can't say I fault Nalini Singh for writing a book about an interesting charac</span>
  <span id="freeText15092719236241567857" style="display:none">Before I wrote a review on this book, I had to sleep on it. I was trying to figure out a way to express my feelings about Mercy. She annoyed the crap out of me for the majority of this book. I felt so bad about it. I love strong women. I am definitely a reader who wants a strong, independent heroine in a story, yet I like the sweet heroines as well. I just like well-written heroines. Mercy was certainly well-written. I can't say I fault Nalini Singh for writing a book about an interesting character like Mercy. Having said that, she really worked my nerves.<br /><br />It suddenly came to me as an epiphany about Mercy. She's a female cat. As a lifelong cat lover, I have made an observation that other cat lovers will probably agree with me on. Female cats can be a pain in the butt. They are much more grumpy and unreasonable more often than male cats. They are mercurial as all get out, one minute wanting to be loved on, the next trying to scratch your eyes out. That's Mercy in a nutshell.<br /><br />Frankly I was doubting for some period of time while I was reading that she deserved Riley. I felt like I was being a sexist thinking this. I asked myself why do I love heroes that are flawed, but Mercy was bugging me. Well, I came to realize that her imperfection wasn't the problem. It was the fact that she gave Riley hell most of the time for what seemed like no good reason. Sometimes she was a purring kitten, but most of the time, not so much. It was made clear fairly often that this was the way of a dominant female changeling, and that was when the lightbulb about female cats came to me. Once I accepted this realization, I could deal with Mercy a lot better. And since Riley loved her for who she was, I guess I can't afford to lose sleep about it.<br /><br />I do have to say that she did admit when she was wrong, most of the time. But she really put Riley through her paces, and he was clearly the one who gave of himself much more. When it came down to it, she made a very difficult choice out of love for him, and I had to give her props for that.<br /><br />Now I have to say that I loved Riley to bits. Nothing wrong with him. The part where he so-called betrayed Mercy, I can acknowledge that it was the wrong decision, but he made it for what he truly believed was the right reason. Just like Mercy couldn't change her spots, if you will forgive the pun. It's wrong to ask a wolf to shed his skin. He had the right to be the dominant male, just like she had the right to be a dominant female. I don't like double standards, so I don't think that Mercy should have been able to get away with her bad behavior (because of her nature) and then give Riley a hard time for him following his nature. I thought that the romance between Riley and Mercy was good reading, although I didn't love it as much as Sascha/Lucas, Vaughn/Faith, Judd/Brenna, and my favorite Dorian/Ashaya. I think it's because I love the Changeling/Psy relationship dynamic so much. Having said that, it was nice to see the hero be a wolf. Love me some wolf heroes. :)<br /><br />Gender politics dealt with, I really enjoyed the suspense and conspiracy elements. Singh writes a great romance, but she also weaves an interesting read that I believe would appeal to a straight science fiction fan if that person didn't mind a lot of kissy-poo along with it. The stakes have been raised, and the world of the Psy/Changeling has expanded to focus more on the human quotient. It will be interesting to see how that aspect plays out in the future. Can I say I am a serious fangirl of the Psy. They are kickbutt. Still want to read more about the Tk-Psy and the Arrows. (Hint, hint, Ms. Singh). <br /><br />As for Hawke and Sienna, I am a little worried how things ended with them. Call me sexist, but I hope that she doesn't get deeply involved with Kit. I want her to wait for Hawke. Don't give up hope, Sienna. Hawke has deep feelings for you, girl. <br /><br />I loved the glimpses of my favorite male character (although I dearly love Dorian and Judd) in this, Hawke. He's just droolicious. More Hawke please.<br /><br />So, I must say that I was not disappointed, although Mercy gave me some heartburn.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15092719236241567857" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

  <span id="freeText17989418977006726032" style="display:none">My favorite of this series so far! But, they also have a huge attraction for each other and have to work together a lot because of their packs' alliance.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443860696i/16423076.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Their romance is really fun because they are both alpha animals. <div id="review_124090401" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/124090401" />
    <a title=" Lady Jayne *~*The Beach Bandida*~*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1453659-lady-jayne-the-beach-bandida"><img alt=" Lady Jayne *~*The Beach Bandida*~*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1295034921p2/1453659.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/124090401?book_show_action=true">Sep 30, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Lady Jayne *~*The Beach Bandida*~*" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Lady Jayne *~*The Beach Bandida*~*" href="/user/show/1453659-lady-jayne-the-beach-bandida"> Lady Jayne *~*The Beach Bandida*~*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1453659-lady-jayne-the-beach-bandida?shelf=owned-read">owned-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1453659-lady-jayne-the-beach-bandida?shelf=romance-paranormal">romance-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1453659-lady-jayne-the-beach-bandida?shelf=author-nalini-singh">author-nalini-singh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1453659-lady-jayne-the-beach-bandida?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer124090401" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14133120852122156048"><b>5 Stars!!</b> - <b>YOWZA!!! I felt Branded by Fire, alright!!!</b><br/><br/>September 2011 - Review to come... But just a few thoughts, for now... This is probably my favourite of the series, so far, along with Dorian's and Ashaya's book and the first book with Lucas and Sascha (which will always have a special place in my heart). I adore the DarkRiver alpha couple. *sighs* And I loved Mercy and Riley. LOVING this series!!!<br/>......<br/><br/>March 2012 - Finally wrote my review.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>Also reviewed at: <a href='http://ladyjaynesreadingden.blogspot.com.au/2012/03/review-branded-by-fire-6-pasy.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lady Jayne's Reading Den</a></i>
</b><br/><br/><b>This </b></span>
  <span id="freeText14133120852122156048" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars!!</b> - <b>YOWZA!!! I felt Branded by Fire, alright!!!</b><br><br>September 2011 - Review to come... But just a few thoughts, for now... This is probably my favourite of the series, so far, along with Dorian's and Ashaya's book and the first book with Lucas and Sascha (which will always have a special place in my heart). I adore the DarkRiver alpha couple. *sighs* And I loved Mercy and Riley. LOVING this series!!!<br>......<br><br>March 2012 - Finally wrote my review.<br><br><b>
  <i>Also reviewed at: <a href="http://ladyjaynesreadingden.blogspot.com.au/2012/03/review-branded-by-fire-6-pasy.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Lady Jayne's Reading Den</a></i>
</b><br><br><b>This installment of the Psy-Changeling series started out <i>SCORCHINGLY HAWT!</i></b> <br><br>When Mercy Smith, a sentinel of the DarkRiver leopard pack, leaves her best friend Dorian’s wedding to go for a run, as it was difficult seeing him and the other sentinels all happily mated, she is found by none other than the highest ranking Lieutenant SnowDancer wolf who pushes her buttons, the sexy Riley Kincaid. Riley can see that Mercy is in heat and antagonises her into a “wrestling” match that turns into something primal…all in the first few pages! As I said, YOWZA!!!<br><br><i>
  <b>Who you calling hot, wolf???</b>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380340019i/696573.jpg" width="230" height="340" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380340019i/696574.jpg" width="320" height="220" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><p>
  <br>
  <i>
    <b>Yield to me, kitty. You know you want to.</b>
  </i>
  <br>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380340019i/696575.jpg" width="260" height="340" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380340019i/696576.jpg" width="250" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
</p><p><br><b>This is the first changeling-changeling romance in the series, and I must say, it was certainly EXPLOSIVE! The chemistry and sparks between Mercy and Riley is off the charts.</b><br><br>This is also the first book with a wolf hero. While I love the DarkRiver cats, I also enjoy getting more of the SnowDancer wolves. And while I’ve loved the stories with the Psy/Changeling and Psy/Human pairings, it was great that Nalini Singh changed pace with this one. <br><br>Mercy and Riley, as the representatives for each of their packs in their still new alliance, are thrown together often, and in this one, they have to work very closely together.<br><br>Mercy a.k.a. Miss Bikini Babe 2067 is afraid she’ll never mate, because she’s a dominant female in her pack and she doesn’t want to be with someone she is more dominant over nor does she want to submit. Mercy is kickass, and her family and pack are very important to her.<br><br><i><b> Miss Bikini Babe 2067 - Rawr!!!</b></i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380340019i/696577._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="380" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Riley a.k.a. The Wall…or Mr Mud Stick/Muddie, as Mercy refers to him … is responsible and serious but is also so deliciously sexy and caring. I love these kinds of heroes! Just like my darling Marcus, Lord Westcliff, of Lisa Kleypas Wallflowers series. They are so outwardly controlled, but when they fall for a woman, their control is decimated and their passions are incredible to behold. Riley is so protective and he has a big heart. Just love him!</p><blockquote>
  <i>“Be gentle with him, Mercy. He's got a heart as big as Texas— he'll die for you without blinking. But he doesn't expect anyone to do the same for him.”</i>
</blockquote> <b>Be gentle, Mercy!</b><i>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380340019i/696578.jpg" width="390" height="420" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
</i><br><br>Physically, these two are far from gentle with each other. Being changelings, biting and scratching certainly factors into their passions - it was very primal. They simply can’t keep their paws off each other.<br><br>On the emotional front, Riley is convinced he wants a domestic female for a mate, not an independent, kickass one, who would be putting herself in danger on a regular basis. But when things develop deeper with Mercy, he realises that Mercy is the one for him. But how can Mercy bring herself to submit to Riley?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380340019i/696579.jpg" width="380" height="280" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>[Edit: Or in Karla's mind....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380340019i/696580._SX540_.jpg" width="380" height="260" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>LMAO! Love ya, Karla sweetie! ^_^]<br> <br><b>I absolutely loved their banter!</b> <blockquote>
  <i>Riley: "Do you want to claw at me, kitty-cat? Come on." <br>Mercy: "Sorry, I don't beat defenseless puppies.”</i>
</blockquote><b>While there was no slow build-up to their physical relationship, like with couples in previous books - though there was already sexual tension brewing between them, earlier in the series - I loved reading about the development of Mercy and Riley's emotional relationship.</b> These two struggled with how to make not only a relationship between two dominants work but between two different changeling packs. <br><br><b>Things aren’t easy for Mercy and Riley, and as much as I enjoyed the banter, I loved the moments of intimacy as they both bared their souls, making this a truly satisfying read. And when they submit to each other, in the end, it was simply wonderful!</b><blockquote>
  <i>“I have something for you.” <br>“Yeah? What? Is it shiny?” <br>They both waited until Indigo had jogged away before resuming their conversation. “So,” Riley asked, “what have you got for me?” <br>Taking his hand, she placed it palm-down over her heart. It would hurt like a bitch, she thought, but he was hers to protect as much as she was his. “Me.” And she opened up her soul, laid herself bare.”</i>
</blockquote> *sighs*<br><br><b>I loved seeing Mercy and Riley get their HEA!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380340019i/696581.jpg" width="230" height="330" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380340019i/696582._SY540_.jpg" width="310" height="390" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love how Nalini Singh lets readers into the ongoing relationships of couples from earlier books after they get their HEA, such as with Lucas and Sascha, who hold a very special place in my heart, and the development that happens in this installment was just “Awww…”. And seeing Judd and Brenna in their HEA, too, was great.<br><br>Sienna is all grown up now and tensions are rising between Sienna and Hawke. Looking forward to getting to their book! <br><br>I enjoyed meeting Mercy’s three gorgeous brothers – Bastian, Sage and Grey.<br><br>I’m enjoying the progression of the overall series story arc and the tensions growing between the Psy, Changelings and humans.<br><br>The mystery of The Ghost continues to intrigue me. <br><br>And is it wrong that I find Kaleb Krychek alluring in some dark way? Could he be The Ghost??<br><br><b>If you still haven’t picked up a Psy-Changeling book by Nalini Singh, then you really should do something about that!</b><br><br>Credits: <br>My Mercy - Amanda Righetti<br>My Riley - Aaron O'Connell<br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~<br><br><b>Psy-Changeling Series Reading Order:</b><br><br>1. Slave to Sensation – (<a>Review here</a>)<br>1.5 "The Cannibal Princess" - Free short story:<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.nalinisingh.com/freebies.php#princess">http://www.nalinisingh.com/freebies.p...</a> - (<a>Review here</a>)<br>2. Visions of Heat - (<a>Review here</a>)<br>3. Caressed By Ice - To be reviewed. <br>4. Mine to Possess (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/124090396" rel="nofollow noopener">Review here</a>) <br>5. Hostage to Pleasure - (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/124090399" rel="nofollow noopener">Review here</a>) <br>5.5 "A Gift for Kit" - Free short story: <br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.nalinisingh.com/freebies.php#gift">http://www.nalinisingh.com/freebies.p...</a><br>6. Branded By Fire - Reviewed.<br>7. Blaze of Memory - To be reviewed.<br>8. Bonds of Justice - To be reviewed.<br>9. Play of Passion<br>10. Kiss of Snow<br><br>And there are also stand-alone novellas:<br>1. "Beat of Temptation" in An Enchanted Season<br>2. "Stroke of Enticement" in The Magical Christmas Cat<br>3. "Whisper of Sin" in Burning Up<br><br>But if you wish to read in strict chronological order, see Nalini Singh's website (link to the page here): <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.nalinisingh.com/psybehind.php">http://www.nalinisingh.com/psybehind.php</a><br><br><br><i>COPYRIGHT DISCLAIMER: I do not hold the copyright to any of the images used in this review. They are posted to add visuals to the review and for fun. If any of these images are yours and you would like me to remove them, please let me know, and I will do so as soon as possible. If I can identify the copyright, I will do so.</i><br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/41975135?book_show_action=true">Jan 05, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="MelissaB" class="user" itemprop="url" name="MelissaB" href="/user/show/1320046-melissab">MelissaB</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">fans of great romances!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=favorite-romances">favorite-romances</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=shapeshifters">shapeshifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=best-heroes">best-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=2017-reads">2017-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=favorite-paranormal-romance">favorite-paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=psy-changling-series">psy-changling-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=2009-reads">2009-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=paper-books-i-own">paper-books-i-own</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer41975135" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1038349079375231627">Branded by Fire starts out with some fireworks as Mercy, a top sentinel in the Dark River leopard pack, has a hot forbidden interlude with Riley, the second to the alpha of the Snow Dancer wolf pack. She is a dominant alpha female in her pack which makes her fear that she will never find a mate because she would need someone more dominant than her and she doesn’t think she would be able to submit to a mate the way she would need to. Riley is a stubborn, protective, by-the-rules man who is helple</span>
  <span id="freeText1038349079375231627" style="display:none">Branded by Fire starts out with some fireworks as Mercy, a top sentinel in the Dark River leopard pack, has a hot forbidden interlude with Riley, the second to the alpha of the Snow Dancer wolf pack. She is a dominant alpha female in her pack which makes her fear that she will never find a mate because she would need someone more dominant than her and she doesn’t think she would be able to submit to a mate the way she would need to. Riley is a stubborn, protective, by-the-rules man who is helplessly drawn to Mercy’s fiery personality. He grew up taking care of his younger siblings and is now the highest ranking lieutenant in the Snow Dancer pack, so he can’t imagine having a mate like Mercy who insists on taking care of herself.<br /><br />Mercy and Riley are thrown together often as their respective pack’s representative in the alliance between the cats and wolves – especially now as attacks on humans, changelings and Psy are beginning to escalate. The sexual attraction between Mercy and Riley leads them to start a forbidden affair because they just can’t keep their hands off each other. Mercy knows Riley is a dominant wolf who will try to take over her life, which she thinks will kill a part of herself. Riley feels like he needs to protect those he loves, especially after what he sees as a failure to protect his little sister Brenna from being attacked. Mercy and Riley start to care a lot about each other but both are afraid of the consequences of staying together. They both dedicate their lives to protecting their packs – plus cats and wolves just barely get along. Can they both survive a mating – and do they have any choice but to try since their feelings are so intense?<br /><br />I loved this story! Mercy and Riley were such a great pair, they really complemented each other in every way. The love scenes were scorching hot! Riley certainly knows how to please a woman. Both Riley and Mercy had to come to terms with each other – Riley had to accept that he could be dominant with Mercy while they were making love but he needed to see her as a partner at all other times and not try to shield her, while Mercy had to accept and trust Riley enough to allow him completely into her heart as a mate.<br /><br />The storyline of the series progresses as we learn more about the battle for and against Silence in the Psy web and more clues about the Ghost’s identity. Sienna and Hawke have small parts in the story, I can’t wait until we see what happens between them. Lucas and Sascha receive wonderful news that I have been waiting for! I also found out the answer to the two questions I have been wondering about since I heard of the pairing between Riley and Mercy: What type of children will a wolf and cat have together and how can two dominant sentinels from different packs actually make a mating work – but you will have to read Branded by Fire to find out for yourself!<br /><br />The Psy/Changling series is one of my favorite romance series, every single book has been amazing. Nalini Singh is a very talented author who writes wonderful romances with a great background story. I highly recommend this series to any romance reader!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1038349079375231627" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_45232508" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/45232508" />
    <a title="Dina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1918270-dina"><img alt="Dina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460302951p2/1918270.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/45232508?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dina" href="/user/show/1918270-dina">Dina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1918270-dina?shelf=series-psy-changeling">series-psy-changeling</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1918270-dina?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1918270-dina?shelf=to-blog">to-blog</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer45232508" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11686238351223198654">I've been struggling with this review since yesterday, trying to figure out why this book didn't earn a 5-star rating from me. I loved Riley, I liked Mercy, I enjoyed the plot and the new developments in the series' story arc - especially the introduction of Bowen, a new secondary character with all the signs of a future hero - and, last but not least, Hawke (oh, how I love thee!) had some major scenes that had me drooling all over the pages. So what was "wrong" with this latest installment in t</span>
  <span id="freeText11686238351223198654" style="display:none">I've been struggling with this review since yesterday, trying to figure out why this book didn't earn a 5-star rating from me. I loved Riley, I liked Mercy, I enjoyed the plot and the new developments in the series' story arc - especially the introduction of Bowen, a new secondary character with all the signs of a future hero - and, last but not least, Hawke (oh, how I love thee!) had some major scenes that had me drooling all over the pages. So what was "wrong" with this latest installment in the <b>Psy-Changeling</b> series?<br /><br />After some pondering, I finally nailed it... I'm afraid to say Riley and Mercy's relationship didn't work too well for me. I mean, they fit each other, I was happy to see them together and, always a plus, their love scenes were hot, but here's the problem: there was no sexual tension and no real build-up to their relationship. They were doing the "panting and sweating" right from the start - and what a 1st Chapter that was, let me tell you! - and, while I understood the reasoning behind it, it ended up "killing" the fun of watching them finding their HEA. The old saying is true, anticipation heightens the pleasure... Judd and Brenna took forever to have their 1st love scene in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/458034.Caressed_By_Ice__Psy_Changeling___3_" title="Caressed By Ice (Psy-Changeling, #3) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Caressed By Ice</a> and, boy, when they did... wow, get me a bucket of ice! But I digress... The thing is, I prefer seeing my H/h working their way towards a sexual relationship, so the Changeling-Changeling pairing in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5628753.Branded_by_Fire__Psy_Changelings___6_" title="Branded by Fire (Psy-Changelings, #6) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Branded by Fire</a> fell kind of flat.<br /><br />Everything else was perfect, including the darn twist Ms. Singh gave to Hawke and Sienna's relationship, and I'm still a devoted fan of the <b>Psy-Changeling</b> series. I'm a bit wary of the next book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6353014.Blaze_of_Memory__Psy_Changeling___7_" title="Blaze of Memory (Psy-Changeling, #7) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Blaze of Memory</a>, because I still can't picture Dev Santos, a secondary character who only appeared in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1830755.Mine_to_Possess__Psy_Changeling___4_" title="Mine to Possess (Psy-Changeling, #4) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Mine to Possess</a> so far, as the hero but, WTH, I trust Ms. Singh to make it work.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11686238351223198654" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1755898439" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Choko" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27962805-choko"><img alt="Choko" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475642755p2/27962805.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1755898439?book_show_action=true">Sep 13, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Choko" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Choko" href="/user/show/27962805-choko">Choko</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1755898439" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14422257190901784961"><b>*** 4.25 ***<br/><br/>A buddy read with Jo and Angela at the PNR hot corner of BB&B </b><br/><br/>Wow!!! I have to say - Nalini not only knows how to create an imaginative and fascinating world, but she can create a chemistry between her characters that sizzles and sets the pages on fire!!! <br/><br/>In the cold world of Psy and the hot world of the Changelings, the Humans have been relegated to a tertiary place in the world order. ANd not surprisingly, they resent it. Beginning with the previous book, the Human Alliance has got</span>
  <span id="freeText14422257190901784961" style="display:none"><b>*** 4.25 ***<br /><br />A buddy read with Jo and Angela at the PNR hot corner of BB&amp;B </b><br /><br />Wow!!! I have to say - Nalini not only knows how to create an imaginative and fascinating world, but she can create a chemistry between her characters that sizzles and sets the pages on fire!!! <br /><br />In the cold world of Psy and the hot world of the Changelings, the Humans have been relegated to a tertiary place in the world order. ANd not surprisingly, they resent it. Beginning with the previous book, the Human Alliance has gotten involved in trying to remap the power structure. Unfortunately, other players might be interested in controlling them in order to achieve their own goals. And whoever it is, is not playing fair - compulsion, abduction, explosion, political manipulation and murder are all on the table and our favorite Wolf and Big Cat Packs are trying to protect and survive with the least innocents being lost in the cross-fire... <br /><br />Enter our Cat Sentinel Mercy and the Wolf Pack Liaison to the Cats, Lieutenant Riley Kincaid. They have worked together for a while and the tension between them is palpable... Until the moment it explodes in some very intense and sizzling skin to skin action!!! Wow! I am sure this much chemistry is illegal! But they come from different packs, old hostilities still resonating in the packs fragile alliance... And a Cat slumming with a Wolf??? Oooo, the horror!!! <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"... “Mercy laughed. “You have to excuse them—boys suffer from an incurable disability.” <br />“What?” <br />“Testosterone.”..."</i>
</b><br /><br />Needles to say, the families will have their say, the job will be an issue, and loyalties will be questioned. However, Riley is determined and the Cat inside Mercy is in danger of being tamed... <br /><br />Al always, I enjoyed the romance a ton, but more than that, I love the constant details we get in small doses each book about the Silence Program, The Psy Net, and the way they have affected each-other, thus changing the world as a whole. I am so intrigued to find out who certain characters are, what their true missions are, and only far behind come the different romantic parings. But it sure feels good to have some nice sexual tension and satisfying outcomes the said tension ends up leading to:):):) It sure is fun to read some good PNR from time to tine:):):) Doing it and doing it Old School! I can't believe I waited so long to read this series - thank you, Joanita and Angela, for nudging me on the way! Love you guys! <br /><br />Now I wish all of you Happy Reading and may you always find Joy in the pages of a good Book!!! <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14422257190901784961" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

</a> is being released soon I felt that a reread was in order.<br><br><s>Three</s> Five “Wildfire &amp; Solid, Rooted Earth” Stars. <br><br><b> The first time I read Mercy &amp; Riley's story I said the following;<br><br>"Up until I love every single book of this series and they all have a rating of at least 4 &amp; 5 Stars. This one unfortunately and it was a tough choice to make."<br><br>The second time around I can truly say that getting to know these two while rereading the other books has given me a better understanding of how these two work and how well they are together. <br><br>It is the year 2080 and the silent war is still being fought. Between the Psy and the Changelings. But there is a factor that they hadn’t taken into consideration. The humans or in this case the Human Alliance. <br><br>Be it humans, Psy or Changelings neither likes change. But is some cases change can kill. Devastate. Destroy.<br><br>The animals are rising and the tides are turning and they aren’t to be underestimated. <br><br>The SnowDancers and the DarkRiver have become allies, they have an understanding and now they have a blood bond. The liaisons between the packs is Mercy, a DarkRiver sentinel and Riley, a SnowDancer Lieutenant. <br><br>In Dorian and Ashaya’s book we know what Mercy is going through. Cats crave touch and they need the most intimate of touch. Mercy hasn’t been getting what she needs though. Everyone is settling down and she also wants to settle down. As a dominant female is is hard for her to let her guard down.<br><br>"I know. Do you think I don't know?" She thrust her hands through her hair. "Damn it Dorian! It's getting to the point where I'm starting to wonder if some of the wolves would be good in bed. [...]<br><br>"Cat and wolf isn't a ... um ... normal combination."<br><br>"And Psy and cat is?" She made a face at him. "Yeah, yeah I know. Cat and wolf is strange." [...]<br><br>Riley and Mercy had their problems at the beginning but that is all foreplay that leads up to the mating dance. <br><br>The first time around I also said this;<br><br>"There were a couple of times where I didn’t want to continue the book. My issue was that I was frustrated. But this was due to the fact that they have been antagonists for so long. So I didn’t quite see how the push and pull would work out."<br><br>My opinion on this has obviously changed as that is what made these two really have something special that all though they antagonised one another they both bent but didn't break. <br><br>Riley suffered from the loss of his parents, being a father to Drew and Brenna and feeling as if he let Brenna down in what happened to her. He keeps a tight reign on his emotions that bothers Mercy to no end. <br><br>I adore Riley with his strength and persistence of Mercy and the lengths he went to, to get his mate. <br><br>As I said Mercy is a strong dominant female she fears that she won’t find a worthy male for her and her cat. But she also doesn't want to loose her tie to her pack which would most likely happen if they completed the mating. Her Gran throws in the complication of swinging some males at her which makes Riley <s>jealous</s>overprotective. <br><br>Mercy is the best. Loyal, fair, tender at times and a mate that she deserves. But she is unsure of the situation. Mercy decides to talk about her issues with Sascha. <br><br>Mercy reached up to redo her ponytail. “You know how predatory changeling men are.”<br><br>“You’re hardly a cream puff.” Sascha’s expression filled with mischief. <br><br>I'm not big on sex/smut at the moment and where I felt the chemistry between them and all in all I enjoyed them as a couple it wasn't over the top. <br><br>“A hand in her hair, wrenching back her head. “What's my name?"<br><br>She scratched trails down his back. He didn't even wince. "My name, kitty. Say my name."<br><br>"Mr. Mud Stick, Muddie for short," she said, even as she rubbed herself against the hard thrust of his denim-covered erection, the roughness of the fabric an exquisite sensation. She would've liked naked skin even more, but he wasn't budging.<br><br>"Say it, or no cock for you today."<br><br>Her mouth fell open. "Fuck you."<br><br>"You'll be doing that shortly.”<br><br>They like to play both as humans and as animals. <br><br>“You said I could pet you as long as I liked.” <br>“Didn't say I wouldn't try to fuck you in the middle of the petting.” <br>Her eyes snapped up to meet his. “That's feline logic. You're a wolf.” <br>“I'm learning from the best.”<br><br>I love how we still get to see interaction between other members of the pack. <br><br>“You should sit,” Lucas said, and he wasn't talking to Mercy.<br><br>Sascha stared at him. “I didn't realize pregnancy of four weeks' duration made me incapable of standing upright.”<br><br>“It makes me incapable of reason.”<br><br>This book will not dishearten me though I will continue with the series. True but I'm going to skip the next two books as they were kind of meh for me.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="4078938663926245571" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Shawna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1802746-shawna"><img alt="Shawna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1574172018p2/1802746.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/48127316?book_show_action=true">Mar 03, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shawna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shawna" href="/user/show/1802746-shawna">Shawna</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">PNR Fans</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Shawna by: </span>
      Several GR friends
  </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer48127316" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9272357000095979878">5 stars – Paranormal Romance<br/><br/>Nalini Singh delivers yet another exceptional addition to the superb <i>Psy-Changeling</i> series. I’ve read all of the six (currently released) books in the series over the past couple of weeks, and it’s amazing that they keep getting better each time and that there are still so many wondrous possibilities for the future. One of the main things that makes this series so fantastic is the terrific balance of unique, spellbinding world building and steamy, sensual romance betw</span>
  <span id="freeText9272357000095979878" style="display:none">5 stars – Paranormal Romance<br /><br />Nalini Singh delivers yet another exceptional addition to the superb <i>Psy-Changeling</i> series. I’ve read all of the six (currently released) books in the series over the past couple of weeks, and it’s amazing that they keep getting better each time and that there are still so many wondrous possibilities for the future. One of the main things that makes this series so fantastic is the terrific balance of unique, spellbinding world building and steamy, sensual romance between strong, passionate characters. <br /><br />This time, the story centers on the H/H pairing of two dominant, powerful, strong-willed alpha changelings, rather than a Psy/human and changeling union, which in my opinion raised the heat factor by about 50+ degrees! <b>Branded by Fire</b> is a very fitting title because this one is a serious scorcher and the most erotic of the books so far...I’m talking scalding HOT! <br /><br />DarkRiver sentinel leopard Mercy is feeling a bit left out and lonely now that so many of her close pack members and fellow sentinels have been mated, not to mention suffering from increased sexual frustration and a raging, unsatiated libido. But being a tough, dominant, alpha female sentinel fighter with a high ranking status in the pack means slim pickins’ in the man/cat and mate department. So what’s a kitty-cat to do? I mean, she’s gotta scratch her itch, right?<br /> <br />Lieutenant Riley Kincaid is second in command among the SnowDancer wolf pack and is tasked with working alongside Mercy to strengthen the DarkRiver and SnowDancer alliance and to solve a string of murders in their territories. He’s extremely attracted to Mercy and wants her, as both a wolf and a man, and for more than just a quickie roll on the forest floor. But getting her to agree won’t be easy, and he knows she’ll never submit to a powerful, dominating, alpha like him who’s used to calling all the shots. And that’s exactly what he wants, a mate who he can protect and that will keep the home den lights burning. Not to mention that Mercy is appalled by the idea of bedding down with a dirty dog, especially one as infuriating as Riley, who seems to live to push her buttons and drive her crazy. But he sure seems to make her inner cat purr in utter delight.<br /><br />He’s a wolf, she’s a cat and both are used to being in charge and on top, but when fire and passion ignites and burns hot between them; can two dominant alphas find a way to submit their hearts? Or will their intense, volatile attraction and all consuming affair endanger the fragile, precious alliance of their packs?<br /><br />Riley and Mercy’s relationship is one of my favorites of the series so far, and the romance in this is definitely the hottest...Yowza! Some of the scenes just about “branded” my fingertips! I loved Riley’s teasing, flirty way with Mercy...very funny and sexy! “<i>Got an itch, kitty?</i>” I loved it! Another excellent read in a phenomenal series! If you’re a paranormal, sci-fi/fantasy romance fan and haven’t yet started on this series, then what are you waiting for? 5 stars!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9272357000095979878" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer449982755" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8736075267007377821"><p>
  <i>Re-reading my favorite series again ;-)</i>
</p> <p>12/09/2016 Buddy reading my favorite series with the wonderful Choko and Angela! </p> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “But sometimes, the human heart loves so deeply that it overcomes the objections of the animal.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <p>Things have been peaceful lately for the DarkRiver cats and the SnowDancer wolves. But they knew it wouldn’t last and when a changeling researcher is kidnapped, Mercy a DarkRiver Sentinel and Riley a SnowDancer lieutenant must work together to find him before it’s</p></span>
  <span id="freeText8736075267007377821" style="display:none"><p>
  <i>Re-reading my favorite series again ;-)</i>
</p> <p>12/09/2016 Buddy reading my favorite series with the wonderful Choko and Angela! </p> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “But sometimes, the human heart loves so deeply that it overcomes the objections of the animal.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <p>Things have been peaceful lately for the DarkRiver cats and the SnowDancer wolves. But they knew it wouldn’t last and when a changeling researcher is kidnapped, Mercy a DarkRiver Sentinel and Riley a SnowDancer lieutenant must work together to find him before it’s too late. </p> <p>Other strange happenings are also occurring across the globe: Psy’s acting out of character, killing others or themselves. Is there a sinister plot at work, or are some Psy’s just losing control? Could this be the work of the Psy Council who is power hungry and intent on stopping the rebels who wants to put a stop to their ruling and Silence, or could it be the work of the newest threat, the Human Alliance, who has no problem using violence? </p> <blockquote>
  <i> “Damn it, Riley. This’ll leave us both broken in the end.”<br />“And is fighting it any less painful?” </i>
</blockquote> <p>And when Mercy and Riley uncovers a dangerous conspiracy, they have to get to the bottom of what is happening before more people die. They also have to decide whether submitting to the passion that burns between them is worth all it could cost. </p> <blockquote>
  <i>She shouldn’t have provoked him, but she couldn’t help herself. It was like he was catnip. One sniff and she lost her mind. </i>
</blockquote> <p>I have loved the tough and feisty Mercy since the first book. Watching all the dominant males in her pack finding their mates has made her worried that she would never find a mate of her own, one that her leopard would be able to accept. And she can’t understand the sudden attraction she feels to the broody and serious wolf. </p> <blockquote>
  <i>To deal with her, to be with her, he’d had to unleash the wolf. He didn’t like being out of control. But neither did he plan on letting Mercy ignore the inferno between them.</i>
</blockquote> <p>Riley loves responsibility and rules and he’s always in control of his emotions. Ever since the suffering his baby sister experienced at the hands of a monster, the guilt and failure he feels has made him even more somber. But no one drives him crazier than the rule breaker Mercy. She’s everything he doesn’t want in a mate, a sentinel who is always in dangerous situations, and one he cannot control. But resisting her is impossible. </p> <blockquote>
  <i>“You didn’t answer my question.”<br />“And you didn’t turn into a puff of smoke and disappear. The world is full of disappointments.”<br />A low growl filled the vehicle. </i>
</blockquote> <p>I absolutely loved the banter between these two. Both are so dominant and refuse to submit to the other, and the sparks between them was addictive. </p> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>He nipped her again. Sharp. Sexy. “You make me so fucking insane, I want to mark you all over. So everyone knows you’re mine.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <p>No one writes better romance for me than Nalini Singh. And the romance is this book was …. FANTASTIC! It was sexy, romantic, so very passionate, and I adored them together. I love how Mercy teased Riley, how she forced him to let go of that rigid control of his and also how protective she was over him. And Riley, I love this sexy wolf and how possessive and protective he was over Mercy. And how he had no problem grovelling when he made mistakes. </p> <blockquote>
  <i>Love. Happiness. Joy. What did any of that matter when the flip side was murderous rage, blood-soaked anarchy? The Psy preferred to leave such things to the “animal” races—and while the humans and changelings buried themselves in the viciousness of emotion, the Psy evolved into the most powerful beings on the planet.<br />Cold. Pitiless. Silent.</i>
</blockquote> <p>The Psy’s struggle with Silence continues, and the Council is still determined that Silence is the best course for the Psy, and some of its members will use any means necessary to keep it implemented and to gain control over all Psy. While the rebels together with the Ghost continue to fight against the Council’s manipulation and control. </p> <blockquote>
  <i> Perhaps Silence was a cage that kept the monsters inside, but it was a cage nonetheless. He knew what it was to grow up inside a cage—a cage so tight, so restrictive that he’d almost forgotten how to breathe. </i>
</blockquote> <p>The Ghost continues to be a mystery to me. With every book, and every little clue we are given about him, my intrigue and love for this unknown rebel grows. </p> <blockquote>
  <i> “I’m the horror in the closet, Sascha, the nightmare even Psy hide from.” </i>
</blockquote> <p>Slowly we are given more insight into the Psy and how they were before Silence took effect. I must say there is a lot of little things I didn’t notice the first time I read this series, but now I can see their importance. The discovery of the E-Psy and what they meant before Silence is slowly being uncovered. I also love learning more about Sascha and her powers. Then there is Sienna Lauren, one of the defected Psy who was taken in by SnowDancer, and one who fears for her powers. I love the animosity between her and Hawke, and I can’t wait to learn more about these two. </p> <p>This is my absolute favorite series of all time. The world and plot building and how this author manages to keep hold of all the different threads that makes up the storyline continues to blow me away. <b>HIGHLY RECOMMENDED</b>.</p></span>
  <a data-text-id="8736075267007377821" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Nalini Singh fans, paranormal romance fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=drinks-on-me">drinks-on-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=king-of-the-harem">king-of-the-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=keep-a-spare-pair-of-knickers">keep-a-spare-pair-of-knickers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=author-nalini-singh">author-nalini-singh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-i-go-rabid-over">books-i-go-rabid-over</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer124825758" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17424974371789480102"><i> Branded by Fire</i> is the perfect title for this book! It’s definitely the hottest of the series so far! Riley, the SnowDancer lieutenant and Mercy, the DarkRiver sentinel are at from the get-go! They are HAWT, HAWT, HAWT!!!<br/><br/>Mercy doesn’t take shit from anyone. It’s one of the reasons why she is so damn good as a sentinel. But with her strength comes scrutiny. Gender roles come into play in this book and even though Riley initially wanted a domestic mate, he can’t seem to stay away from Mercy’s fel</span>
  <span id="freeText17424974371789480102" style="display:none"><i> Branded by Fire</i> is the perfect title for this book! It’s definitely the hottest of the series so far! Riley, the SnowDancer lieutenant and Mercy, the DarkRiver sentinel are at from the get-go! They are HAWT, HAWT, HAWT!!!<br /><br />Mercy doesn’t take shit from anyone. It’s one of the reasons why she is so damn good as a sentinel. But with her strength comes scrutiny. Gender roles come into play in this book and even though Riley initially wanted a domestic mate, he can’t seem to stay away from Mercy’s feline charms.<br /><br />I really liked Mercy, though Tally may still be my favourite heroine. Her take-no-shit attitude rivalled Riley’s and I thought they shared more similarities than differences. It was the main reason why they fought so much. The power play between the two caused a lot of tension, both emotional and sexual and it was a real treat to see them work it out. What I loved about this book is the fact that it’s not simple or easy for the wolf and the cat. They have to work damn hard to make it work.<br /><br />I loved reading about Mercy’s brothers, Bas, Grey, and Sage. They are all so funny and the familial bond that they share is too cute for words. Check out my favourite quote below!<br /><br />We also get caught up with Sascha and Lucas and, can I just say how happy I am about them!? *does happy dance* I love the presence of kids in this series. Whether they are human, changeling or Psy, I love them all! The moments with Sakura and Riley and then Ben and Hawke? Too adorable! Then there’s also Toby, whom I think can really be a major player in the rest of the series.<br /><br />Speaking of children, it seems that Sienna has finally grown up and THANK YOU SINGH for this change! I am dying for some Hawke/Sienna action! I hope nothing happens with Kit and Sienna. Just give Hawke some time, Sienna! I swear he’ll make it up to you!<br /><br />But the real question is....<br /><br /><b>TEAM SNOWDANCER OR TEAM DARKRIVER!?</b><br /><br />I keep flip-flopping between the two! I can’t choose!<br /><br />Bottom line? <i>Branded by Fire</i> is burning hot! I loved it! It’s my second favourite of the series after <i> Mine to Possess</i><br /><br />Favourite Quote:<br />"Should've thought of that before you told my ex-girlfriend I eat live kittens for breakfast." <br /><br />A tiny twinge of guilt. Then the cat wondered what Riley would think of her last successful "shoo-away." "Who knew she'd believe me?" [<br /><br />"Oh no? When you 'accidentally' opened the cupboard to expose my 'kitten cage' full of the poor, sad kitties I was going to snack on?" A raised eyebrow. "Wasn't the cage next to my special 'kitten defurring' tools?" <br /><br />"They were obviously fake." <br /><br />Bas just stared at her.<br /></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Psy Changeling Fans, Nalini Singh fans, paranormal romance fans </span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=shapeshifter">shapeshifter</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=favorite">favorite</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=there-are-hot-men">there-are-hot-men</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=own-mass-market">own-mass-market</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=science-fiction-romance">science-fiction-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer100840003" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17392300163859923109"><b>I'm soooo happy </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380334494i/693757.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>I'd read Branded by Fire before, and I must said this book is one of the best of Psy Changeling series! Beside Play of Passion and Kiss of Snow. What can I said? Kincaid Brothers are sexy as hell and Hawke, their alpha more sexy than hell, LOL!<br/><br/>And Riley and Mercy are my favorite couple beside Elena-Raphael !<br/><br/>So, when Nalini held a contest to support her at DA BWAHA (vote for her book <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6582637.Archangel_s_Kiss__Guild_Hunter___2_' title='Archangel's Kiss (Guild Hunter, #2) by Nalini Singh' rel='nofollow noopener'>

<span id="freeTextContainer7281223581882627285">Book 6 is a Changeling to Changeling pairing. Mercy, a Leopard Changeling and Riley, a Wolf Changeling. <br/><br/>I am loving the progress from story to story. I enjoy seeing past book characters as well as new characters. For such a dominant wolf, Riley was more sensitive than I was expecting. I liked that about him. <br/><br/>Mercy is also a dominant female and unfortunately she came off too hard to me. Her expectations seemed to be really high as well. She wanted a more dominant male but there seemed to be a fin</span>
  <span id="freeText7281223581882627285" style="display:none">Book 6 is a Changeling to Changeling pairing. Mercy, a Leopard Changeling and Riley, a Wolf Changeling. <br /><br />I am loving the progress from story to story. I enjoy seeing past book characters as well as new characters. For such a dominant wolf, Riley was more sensitive than I was expecting. I liked that about him. <br /><br />Mercy is also a dominant female and unfortunately she came off too hard to me. Her expectations seemed to be really high as well. She wanted a more dominant male but there seemed to be a fine line for her expectations of Riley. I guess it was a good thing he had that sensitive side to him that kept him from being too dominant for Mercy.<br /><br />Still very good, I just didn't enjoy Mercy as much as I have past heroines in the series.</span>

<div id="review_90020145" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/90020145" />
    <a title="Beanbag Love" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2598237-beanbag-love"><img alt="Beanbag Love" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1249531311p2/2598237.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/90020145?book_show_action=true">Feb 16, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beanbag Love" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beanbag Love" href="/user/show/2598237-beanbag-love">Beanbag Love</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer90020145" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14352560861996344287">I read this book last week, but I've been so busy I haven't had a chance to review it. In fact, I've already read another two books since. Oh well, better late than never.<br/><br/>I really liked this installment in the Psy-Changeling series. I liked that the relationship took off early in the book ... oh boy, did it ever ... and that the couple was pretty open and honest about their nearly impossible future. <br/><br/>Mercy is a leopard sentinal. Riley is a wolf lieutenant. They've been partnered to watch over a p</span>
  <span id="freeText14352560861996344287" style="display:none">I read this book last week, but I've been so busy I haven't had a chance to review it. In fact, I've already read another two books since. Oh well, better late than never.<br /><br />I really liked this installment in the Psy-Changeling series. I liked that the relationship took off early in the book ... oh boy, did it ever ... and that the couple was pretty open and honest about their nearly impossible future. <br /><br />Mercy is a leopard sentinal. Riley is a wolf lieutenant. They've been partnered to watch over a particular zone between the two packs and they've been bugging each other ever since. <br /><br />Poor Mercy is an alpha, which is very difficult for a female changeling. She would never be satisfied with a submissive mate, but also would never be able to be the 'beta' in a relationship. She's only attracted to alphas but they always want to run the show and a female alpha can't deal with that. It's a very real quandary.<br /><br />One of the things I like about the changelings is that sex is a part of their lives. Touch, sensation, release ... they're all necessary for keeping a lid on their dangerous passions. They can easily lose their humanity if they don't 'git sum' regularly. Which, if you accept that context, takes care of a lot of baggage.<br /><br />Mercy, however, hasn't been 'gittin sum' in far too long. Riley discovers her in the woods in quite a bit of discomfort. Even though they drive each other crazy as working partners, they've been driving each other crazy in a deeper sense as well. So, right there near the beginning of the book we get an explosive, erotic situation that sets the tone for their relationship for the rest of the book. <br /><br />Best of all, it deviates from the template. *does happy dance* <br /><br />Singh does a great job of showing the push and pull of an alpha/alpha relationship very believably. You know they're going to end up together, and you root for it, but you also can't quite figure out how much sacrifice will have to be made and by whom. It's an intriguing story line.<br /><br />Yes, the inter-species love affair feels odd, but changelings mate with humans so it really isn't that far fetched. The problem is mainly two alpha personalities blood-bonded with two separate predatory changeling packs. Sparks do fly.<br /><br />So, this has been my favorite of the series so far. There are some other story lines forwarded and more information is given about the Council so it's a very well rounded reading experience.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14352560861996344287" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4148118-valerie?shelf=audio-reads">audio-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4148118-valerie?shelf=2020-reads">2020-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4148118-valerie?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4148118-valerie?shelf=2018-reads">2018-reads</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1338136677" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6426644541469383820">I so love this series, this author, this book. <br/><br/>I will admit to not loving Mercy as much as Riley. I think it's because they are both so dominate. I felt like I needed to pick a side so I did. Riley. But I love the characters in this book and series. More than the other books in this series, this one spent more time with other characters and I loved it. The surprise for Lucas and Sascha, the moments with Judd, the time with Vaughn and his Red, Faith, -- all so wonderful. I loved it all.<br/><br/>This world</span>
  <span id="freeText6426644541469383820" style="display:none">I so love this series, this author, this book. <br /><br />I will admit to not loving Mercy as much as Riley. I think it's because they are both so dominate. I felt like I needed to pick a side so I did. Riley. But I love the characters in this book and series. More than the other books in this series, this one spent more time with other characters and I loved it. The surprise for Lucas and Sascha, the moments with Judd, the time with Vaughn and his Red, Faith, -- all so wonderful. I loved it all.<br /><br />This world is complex and full. I enjoy how the three groups (humans, shifter, and psy) are intertwined and the story is dynamic. So many bad guys that I don't trust for one minute, so many good guys that are totally part of my pack, so many new characters to meet and get to know, and so many fun, interesting relationships. Makes every book enjoyable and obsessive.<br /><br />Yes, I'm obsessed. As soon as I finish one, I want the next one. And this one ended with a couple interesting little tidbits that have me really wanting to dig into the next.<br /><br />Shifters are my favorite paranormal. And I loved that this book was about two shifters. Previously, we had mixed couples so I was interested to see how I'd feel about two shifters. Of course, one is from each of the major packs. There is definitely some rivalry between the wolves and cats. Mercy calls Riley wolf. He calls her kitty cat. What started as a dig ended as something more. It was interesting to see how these two would come to terms with things. It wasn't an easy road for them and I loved how they figured it out. <br /><br />I will continue to read my obsession. I've been buying up this authors other big series to have on the ready for when this one is complete. Because I don't think this obsession is just for the series but for the author. She mixes incredible world building, full dynamic characters and fascinating stories to hold my interest every time.<br /><br />If you love paranormal romance, then this author, this series needs to be on your short list to read soon.</span>
