<div id="review_582978205" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/582978205" />
    <a title="Angela" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4255477-angela"><img alt="Angela" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398251387p2/4255477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/582978205?book_show_action=true">Apr 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela" href="/user/show/4255477-angela">Angela</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6590314-branded-by-fire">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=review-books-done">review-books-done</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2016-read">2016-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2013-read">2013-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=aoc">aoc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2019-read">2019-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer582978205" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer599388491736485047">This has always been one of my favorite books in this series - I love the dominance of Mercy, and how that plays against the dominance of Riley. I love how committed they both end up being to figuring it out. I love that the romance is effortlessly woven into the plot, and an important part of everything that's going on. I love that there isn't unnecessary drama that bleeds over into the life-and-death things going on in the world.<br/><br/>Plus, Mercy and Riley burn up the pages. I've said in a lot of re</span>
  <span id="freeText599388491736485047" style="display:none">This has always been one of my favorite books in this series - I love the dominance of Mercy, and how that plays against the dominance of Riley. I love how committed they both end up being to figuring it out. I love that the romance is effortlessly woven into the plot, and an important part of everything that's going on. I love that there isn't unnecessary drama that bleeds over into the life-and-death things going on in the world.<br /><br />Plus, Mercy and Riley burn up the pages. I've said in a lot of recent reviews that I'm pretty much over the sex scenes in books - and I think that holds true in the majority of instances - but I can't deny that the scenes between Mercy and Riley, in this book, are off the charts sexy. Part of this is just because of the skill of Nalini Singh in writing a good romance, and part of that is from her ability to weave actual relationship and character building into the sex scenes. They're not unnecessary - yeah, they're fun and sexy and hot to read, but they're also important in the development of the characters singly, and together as a couple. And that makes them even hotter.<br /><br />I've always been fascinated by this world that the Psy, Changelings, and Humans live in, but the world gets ever more intricate the further you get into the series. The ties of friendship and family, the alliances, and pacts built all serve to change the shape of the world. A world that's seeming to move inexorably towards war and destruction. <br /><br />There are so many different factions and people grabbing for power that it's hard to see a peaceful way out of this. When a select few are willing to sacrifice so many for their cause, it makes me despair. But when others work so hard to fight against that? Makes me cheer. This series gives me hope - hope that even those with radically different mindsets, opinions, beliefs, and backgrounds can come together and make a difference for the better.<br /><br />I think that's one thing that I've always loved about the Romance genre in general. The hope. The happiness. The idea that no matter how bad things are, they will get better. And what Nalini's done in this series is show that on a broader scale as well. Not only do the main characters get their HEA, you begin to see that even the more widely disparate individuals can decide that there's a better way.<br /><br />I like that not everything in this series is black-and-white. There are shades of grey. There are characters that aren't exactly good, but maybe they're not exactly who you believed them to be in the first place either. I love how we slowly get to pull back layers on many of these characters. I love how it makes me think critically about motivations and actions taken. I love how even the most (seemingly) cold and Silent characters have moments where their conscious shines through and makes them question. <br /><br />That's the beauty of this series - it started so simply, just one Psy mating to one Changeling. A world where it seems that the power struggle is more about politics than anything else. Now, six books in (as of this review), it's becoming more and more obvious that everything is bigger, means more, and what we thought we knew might not be exactly the case. The stakes are high. <br /><br />I'm invested in this world, in the characters. I've built relationships with these characters, and coming back to re-visit them through re-reads is like coming home.<br /><br />Review also available at <a href="http://thebookeaters.net" rel="nofollow noopener">The Book Eaters</a><br /><br /><br /><br />Original thoughts:<br />Mercy, a DarkRiver leopard Sentinel, and Riley, a SnowDancer wolf Lietenient. Hot damn, do the sparks fly. <br /><br />This is the first book where two changeling-dominant personalities come together. And their relationship starts early in the book, with one of the sexiest scenes in this series to date.<br /><br />Mercy knows she'd never be happy with a submissive for a mate, it's just not the way she's built. She also knows that she couldn't take the 'beta' role in the relationship either. That she might not ever be able to accept a dominant mate. This leaves her with a very real problem. With all the dominant leopards mated, her touch-hunger is nearly out of control. It comes as one hell of a surprise to her that Riley's the one she lets close.<br /><br />Riley's always pictured himself with a submissive mate that sits home - safe and sound. He can't pull himself away from Mercy, though. And as he continues to pursue her - for reasons he doesn't fully understand - you get a much deeper insight into this person nicknamed "The Wall."<br /><br />I loved every minute of this book. Another favorite in the series, it's a pure joy to read. Mercy and Riley are well matched, and I really like how they don't give or take crap from each other. They demand honesty, respect, and because they're both dominant, for each other to come halfway and meet in the middle. It's important to both of them otherwise they could throw away what they're slowly building.<br /><br />This is definitely not one to miss!</span>
  <a data-text-id="599388491736485047" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_62429505" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/62429505" />
    <a title="valee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2320890-valee"><img alt="valee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1443365004p2/2320890.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/62429505?book_show_action=true">Jul 06, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="valee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="valee" href="/user/show/2320890-valee">valee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780575100053" href="/book/show/8820028-branded-by-fire">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2320890-valee?shelf=amazing-pnr-romance">amazing-pnr-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer62429505" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18279714301866144546">5++++++ (How many "+" are allowed?LOL)<br/><b>How could I ever forgot why this is one of my top fav books?!</b> <br/><br/>Seriously, this book was just beyond words, I do understand now why I wasn't able to write a review about it the first time I read it; but now, after reading it for a second time, I just feel like I NEED to do a review. Does that make any sense for you?LOL, it's weird, first I felt I didn't want to write it because I would never be able to show you guys in words how much I felt with this book but </span>
  <span id="freeText18279714301866144546" style="display:none">5++++++ (How many "+" are allowed?LOL)<br /><b>How could I ever forgot why this is one of my top fav books?!</b> <br /><br />Seriously, this book was just beyond words, I do understand now why I wasn't able to write a review about it the first time I read it; but now, after reading it for a second time, I just feel like I NEED to do a review. Does that make any sense for you?LOL, it's weird, first I felt I didn't want to write it because I would never be able to show you guys in words how much I felt with this book but now I just feel like so much is needed to be said about it. This is by far the best book in the series IMHO. I know many don't feel this way and I can understand it because this book wont be as good for everybody. This is one of those books you love or you don't really enjoy, no greys there. I'm definitely in the loving group , even more, I adore and worship this book because from beginning to end it makes me feel so much. So many things I love about it that it's hard to name them, but I'll try so you guys can understand.<br /><br />Sigh**, where to start? First and above everything else, I adore the link and the relationship Mercy and Riley share. From the beginning it was just explosive, they are like dynamite together. It's well known that cats and wolves just don't mate, it's not meant to be, it has happened before but they prefer to mate between their own. Then how can't they help be obsessed about each other? They have known for a while but recently the attraction between each is too strong, they can't keep their hands from each other. From the beginning of the book we see this chemistry hitting the roof, it's so powerful that you can't help to only want to read about them and skip the rest of the pages, even though those pages are amazing as well. Both strong members of their pack, but not totally willing to sacrifice their link to them; but in order to really mate and be together it seems they have to, so how can you choose between your mate, the one person you have been waiting all your life to meet, and your pack, the same people that have given everything for you your whole existence? It's not easy, and all the problems they face are so real that you just suffer with them and wanna help them go through them all so they can be together for once and for all.Riley is such a deep character with so many layers, but above all he is a caring and strong person, one of those who would give everything, and I mean EVERYTHING, to make sure you're happy and ok. To have someone love you so much can make you feel so humble. I assure you guys to read about a hero like this is amazing. Then we have Mercy, which I adore as well, because she is what she is. You will never see her change or flex for anybody. She is so strong for a female, with the best values and so much honour. She loves as much too but it's so hard for her to give that love. If you're gonna read this book you just have to understand that things in it are different. You just can't analyse their actions as a human, you have to see their actions as what they are, changeling actions, based on instinct and the very thing they are and rules them. This is a very complex series and you just can't pick up this book without the bases of the others. <br /><br />This is also the instalment with more information about Sienna and Hawke so it's just impossible not to love it as we have been waiting to read more about them since the beginning. Many surprises and huge turns develop as well. I believe this is the most important book in the series as what plot is concern. Many changes are coming and you can see how things are not gonna be the same any more. The good things is that you just can't imagine what's coming, that's how good NS is. With most series I just know what will happen because they are so predictable, but with NS I never have the slightest idea. Her series is so multifaceted and has so many paths to develop that many things are possible, you just have to keep reading to know more.<br /><br />Guys, <b>I just wont never get tired of telling you that a re-read is fundamental in many levels to really get to love and appreciate this series</b>. There's just not any other series more worth of a re-read. I'm just ecstatic I decided to do it before Hawke's book comes out because now I know I'm ready. I never realized how much about the series I had been missing before now, so listen and make this re-read because it's definitely needed and so worth it, you'll enjoy every second of it.</span>

<div id="review_296443928" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/296443928" />
    <a title="ᴥ Irena ᴥ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5252054-irena"><img alt="ᴥ Irena ᴥ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1425497470p2/5252054.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/296443928?book_show_action=true">Mar 05, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="ᴥ Irena ᴥ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="ᴥ Irena ᴥ" href="/user/show/5252054-irena">ᴥ Irena ᴥ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780575100053" href="/book/show/8820028-branded-by-fire">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5252054-irena?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5252054-irena?shelf=shapeshifters">shapeshifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5252054-irena?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5252054-irena?shelf=short-stories-from-book-series">short-stories-from-book-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer296443928" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12496816705916279901"><br/>There are many things to love in this book. The weakest point (that is not to say it's bad) of it is the romance itself. For me, at least. It's just personal preference. I don't really like characters like Mercy. She took her sweet time to recognize Riley's worth, but I forgive her because of the way she opened up herself. As for Riley, the best description of him was given by his brother. <br/>The rest of the book is all about the beginnings: Nikita's hidden depths, Sienna's designation, Sienna and </span>
  <span id="freeText12496816705916279901" style="display:none"><br />There are many things to love in this book. The weakest point (that is not to say it's bad) of it is the romance itself. For me, at least. It's just personal preference. I don't really like characters like Mercy. She took her sweet time to recognize Riley's worth, but I forgive her because of the way she opened up herself. As for Riley, the best description of him was given by his brother. <br />The rest of the book is all about the beginnings: Nikita's hidden depths, Sienna's designation, Sienna and Hawke, the eagles, Human Alliance and Bowen. And so many other things.<br /><br />***<br /><br />The first time I'd read these books, I focused more on the couple the book features rather than the rest of it. I must admit you shouldn't believe the times it says I read some of these books. I must have read the first one more than a couple of times. I read parts of some of them every now and then. <br />As for <i>Branded by Fire</i>, this <i>is</i> my second time reading it. I appreciate it so much more now. Don't get me wrong, I loved it the first time I'd read it too. However, this time I paid attention to <i>all other</i> things too; things like the subtle foreshadowing of the ugliness and changes to come in the world, the power shifts and more personal changes between various characters. <br /><br />The romance is what you'd expect considering the type of people Mercy and Riley are. They do have to overcome the trust issues. She honestly can't stand being shielded and Riley has to fight the urge to do just that. Their issues are believable and even though the way that particular storyline is resolved may sound naive, I really don't care. Both characters and the way they are dealing with their issues are fun. <br /><i>Branded by Fire</i> is not emotionally charged as most other books. We are dealing with two very stubborn and strong characters. Even with Riley's guilt over Brenna's ordeal, you don't get to see too much sadness. The only time it really got to me as far as these two are concerned is when Drew told Mercy about his big brother - 'He's got a heart as big as Texas - he'll die for you without blinking. But he doesn't expect anyone to do the same for him.'<br /><br />What makes this story even better are those other things I mentioned. I'll list just a couple of them as a reminder (in no particular order). <br />One, a couple of Councillors are working on their own secret agendas and not the one we are used to. That little fact didn't escape the notice of the most powerful (and my favourite) of them. <br />Two, the Human Alliance goes crazy a bit in this book. <br />Three, the author teases us even more with the Ghost. He appears more than once. I loved that character even before I got to his book. ('When the most notorious rebel in the Net broke his Silence, the shield would well and truly shatter'.)<br />Four and the most heartbreaking of all, Sienna Lauren's unravelling. You still don't get to find out what is her designation, but it is mentioned a couple of times in this book. Even Alice Eldridge is mentioned here.<br />Speaking of Alice, that brings me to the book Nikita sent to Sascha. I am still hoping Nikita will get her own story at least in a short story format or a novella. I can only imagine the control and strength this woman had to have to do what she did when she had cut the ties with Sascha in the first book.<br /><br />Anyway, these are just a couple of things I found worth noting. Loved it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12496816705916279901" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1126039984" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18338473295196039075"><b>3.5 stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418250443i/12720860.png' width='400' height='238' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This is not a bad rating, I actually quite enjoyed this book, just not as much as I thought I would. It started off really well, I mean, it was hot and what a great introduction! Sucked me right in. But, after a while, I just found the story lacking. <br/><br/>The love story wasn't as good as usual, sure this time it's two dominant changelings, so I knew it was going to be different, but it was just too different for me, I guess. Riley and Mercy got involved right away and I don't mind that but i</span>
  <span id="freeText18338473295196039075" style="display:none"><b>3.5 stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418250443i/12720860.png" width="400" height="238" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is not a bad rating, I actually quite enjoyed this book, just not as much as I thought I would. It started off really well, I mean, it was hot and what a great introduction! Sucked me right in. But, after a while, I just found the story lacking. <br><br>The love story wasn't as good as usual, sure this time it's two dominant changelings, so I knew it was going to be different, but it was just too different for me, I guess. Riley and Mercy got involved right away and I don't mind that but it got old pretty fast. <br><br>They had sex, they got mad and yelled at each other, they went their separate ways but they couldn't stay away from each other and, <i>ça recommence</i>, sex, fight, separate ways, sex, fight, separate ways... See what I mean? I got bored and annoyed.<br><br>I loved Riley, I really did. How sweet, protective, strong, understanding, hot and funny he was but I didn't like Mercy all that much. She pissed me off. I get it, she's a sentinel, she's a dominant, she's strong and used to have her way but she could be so freaking frustrating and annoying. Ugh. How stubborn can you be?! I liked the fact that she realized her mistakes and apologized, that was good but, seriously, Mercy was definitely not my favorite heroine.<br><br>As usual, loved the secondary characters. So happy for Sascha and Lucas, but I had my doubts already! We get to meet a few new characters, like the Falcons and two luscious leopards from Mercy's grandmother's pack.<br><br>Oh and Sienna and Hawke??! Holy shitoly. <b>I.Want.More.</b> And I have to read 3 more books before, finally, getting their story?! How can I possibly do that?!<br><br>The plot wasn't exceptional either. Another thing I didn't particularly like. It was there but it wasn't awesome, nothing to write home about.<br><br>Still, <b>Branded by Fire</b> was a good book, super hot (the hottest so far, might I add) but it could've been better, for me. I'm definitely not stopping binge reading the <i>Psy-Changeling</i> series! Onto the next.</span>

<div id="review_267675171" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/267675171" />
    <a title="Lisa Kay" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2459470-lisa-kay"><img alt="Lisa Kay" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1534570690p2/2459470.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/267675171?book_show_action=true">Jan 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa Kay" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa Kay" href="/user/show/2459470-lisa-kay">Lisa Kay</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook " href="/book/show/15719683-branded-by-fire">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=m-pb-paperback">m-pb-paperback</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=amazing-secondary-characters">amazing-secondary-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=2012-in-2012-group-challenge">2012-in-2012-group-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=authors-s">authors-s</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=m-audible-dot-com">m-audible-dot-com</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=buddy-read-rlftci">buddy-read-rlftci</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=character-woman-in-pants">character-woman-in-pants</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=genre-shapeshifters">genre-shapeshifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=genre-romance-paranormal">genre-romance-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=series-p">series-p</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer267675171" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1214376356791899097"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379773000i/313800._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>★★★★½ (This is a review of the audiobook.) <b>Angela Dawe</b> continues to narrate the wonderful <i>Psy-Changeling</i> series, and with the sixth book she delivers her usual excellent job of distinguishing the male and female characters. However, I must admit I’m impressed with the way she does the children; there is innocence in her tone that comes across. She is one of the readers I seek out when choosing my next audiobook.<br/><blockquote>
  <i>Willow, a lynx cub who is traumatized when her brother, Nash, a MIT student is kid</i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText1214376356791899097" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379773000i/313800._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>★★★★½ (This is a review of the audiobook.) <b>Angela Dawe</b> continues to narrate the wonderful <i>Psy-Changeling</i> series, and with the sixth book she delivers her usual excellent job of distinguishing the male and female characters. However, I must admit I’m impressed with the way she does the children; there is innocence in her tone that comes across. She is one of the readers I seek out when choosing my next audiobook.<br><blockquote>
  <i>Willow, a lynx cub who is traumatized when her brother, Nash, a MIT student is kidnapped.</i>
  <br>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379772905i/312893.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote>Oh! This is a good one. I wasn’t sure if I was going to like a struggle between two dominants: Sentinel Mercy Smith from the DarkRiver cats, and Lieutenant Riley Kincaid from the SnowDancer wolves. Nonetheless, it was exceptional.<br><br>The chemistry between these two equals is H.O.T. Ms. Singh is deft in handling the love scenes! They certainly sizzle; however, while both individuals like it rough, the interludes are evocative of a deeper emotional tenderness. Oh, yes. Mercy is certainly flirting and cavorting with Riley in what she calls “shoo-away,” but really she’s playing a very dangerous game of “Come here, come here, come here…Go away, go away, go away.” She is definitely getting off on the excitement of the chase. But it is more than that. She wants Riley to prove himself worthy of all she has to offer as a lover; however, I believe there is a part of her that is not aware she really wants him to demonstrate he is worthy of being her mate. Still, these two pack liaisons have a lot of issues to work out. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Where will they live? Will the mating bond cause one to have to leave their family pack? Which will give up their blood-link/sentinel-bond to their Alpha? Can they have kids; will those off-springs be able to shift? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>As deft as this writer is <i>in</i> the bedroom (or forest floor), she’s equally so outside; presenting us with a gripping suspense. Conspiracy is everywhere! There are a lot more clues and few more answers to what has been going on in this series’ story-line: The Ghost, the NetMind, the Human Alliance, the ‘puppet master,’ the Information Merchant, the PsyNet, Pure Psy, the LaurenNet, Henry Scott, Kaleb Krycheck, Anthony Kyriakus, and Nikita Duncan! We get updates on Judd and Brenna, Lucas and Sascha, Hawke and Sienna and so many, many others from this series. <br><br>I often do a great disservice to Ms. Singh; I tend to rate her books against each other instead of against other paranormal romance writers. I’m such a moody reader and it isn’t fair that the next book should have to match my current temperament. But all of her books are a step above other PNR writers.<br><br>If you haven’t started this series, and you enjoy paranormal romances, shifters, and futurist stories, this is a great one to start!<br><br><u> <b> Audiobook Covers</b> </u> <i> <br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10832348.Slave_to_Sensation" title="Slave to Sensation by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow //<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('oJ/m495V92nsyGn/W2fYc2MSF4PffGfGGT1CQQwVfhs39OwpLbziSWyeXEJI2nm4+0yW6BZBGGhWvEFFMnlujQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('5YlHO1fYTmYk7V78swMQDOZdT0a9bWJcIIhNmzjpaYZy4k3xpDFbRqS7a0GgvrHHfgPOLXRQHfJvCU6fBoV5EA==')})
  }
//]]>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer11129993002204443595">I've been writing as long as I can remember and all of my stories always held a thread of romance (even when I was writing about a prince who could shoot lasers out of his eyes). I love creating unique characters, love giving them happy endings and I even love the voices in my head. There's no other job I would rather be doing. In September 2002, when I got the call that Silhouette Desire wanted t</span>
  <span id="freeText11129993002204443595" style="display:none">I've been writing as long as I can remember and all of my stories always held a thread of romance (even when I was writing about a prince who could shoot lasers out of his eyes). I love creating unique characters, love giving them happy endings and I even love the voices in my head. There's no other job I would rather be doing. In September 2002, when I got the call that Silhouette Desire wanted to buy my first book, Desert Warrior, it was a dream come true. I hope to continue living the dream until I keel over of old age on my keyboard.<br /><br /><br />I was born in Fiji and raised in New Zealand. I also spent three years living and working in Japan, during which time I took the chance to travel around Asia. I’m back in New Zealand now, but I’m always plotting new trips. If you’d like to see some of my travel snapshots, have a look at the Travel Diary page (updated every month).<br /><br />So far, I've worked as a lawyer, a librarian, a candy factory general hand, a bank temp and an English teacher and not necessarily in that order. Some might call that inconsistency but I call it grist for the writer's mill.<br /><br /></span>
